<user_id>106820875640851897876<//user_id><name>HairFreek Barbers</name><date>1533902446267</date>< rate>
5<//rate>
< Review>
I was a little worried at first.  We couldn't find parking and it looked closed.  But we made it!
Fast service,  friendly staff,  and the food is the best K BBQ I've had yet!
Adding to my review...
After a second visit,  I like this place even more! It's a different experience.  It's family owned.  Not by a bunch of quiet Koreans,  but a fun Chicano/Latino family.  The decor is artsy,  the music 80's. The menu is set up a little different and after reading these cry baby reviews,  I can answer their complaints.
The least expensive plate is $12.99 and it's all you can eat. The meat flavors are limited on that meal,  but its all you can eat.
We ordered the $18.99 plate. It came with everything you get at those loud Asian run places.  We shared everything.  And it was all you can eat.  It taste just as good,  if not better,  than any Korean run restaurant.

People are just not used to seeing Chicanos serving K food.  Get over it! Enjoy!< /Review>

< text>
Squandered opportunity. Being one of the only kbbq places in Hollywood there is no reason why this place should not have a 2 hour wait on a Saturday night. It all starts with the menu. The cheapest ayce option comes with 2 meats, why even bother putting that on the menu. The banchan selection is very small maybe 4-5 items rice being one of the options. Salad only comes with more expensive ayce options. Next is the sauces. There is some oil and some kind of spicy mayo type sauce on the table, but really doesn't serve the right purpose. Service is also a little slow. Meat wasn't the greatest but not the worst.

I had high hopes, but unfortunately those hopes were shattered.< /text>
